<h1>RANKING BASED ON REVIEW</h1>

</div>

<section id=”about”>

<div class=”section-inner”>

<h2>CREATE RANKING BASED ON REVIEW</h2>

<p>As graduating cohort may face difficulties in choosing their schools during the Covid pandemic, we provide summarised school information and ranking system.</p>

<h3>THE BENEFITS OF OUR WEBPAGE</h3>

<ul>

<li>All information are officially retrieved from the Ministry of Education with detailed subject combination provided in a school</li>

<li>The ranking system is based on alumni's review instead of rank point or academic so that the students have the general idea of the life beyond studying in school</li>

<li>Instead of searching every single school webpage, we can help you save time by providing all the information you need</li>

</ul>

</div>

</section>

<section id=”contact”>

<div class=”section-inner”>

<h2>OUR REVIEW SYSTEM PARTNERSHIP</h2>

<li><a href=”https://www.facebook.com/EduReachServices/“>Facebook</a></li>

</ul>
